<t>CREATE TABLE policy (
    policy_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    policy_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    policy_holder_id INT NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    end_date DATE NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE claim (
    claim_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    policy_id INT NOT NULL,
    claim_date DATE NOT NULL,
    claim_amount DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL
);
</t><s>UPSERT INTO policy (policy_id, policy_type, policy_holder_id, start_date, end_date) VALUES (1, 'Health', 101, '2022-01-01', '2022-12-31') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE policy_type='Health', policy_holder_id=101, start_date='2022-01-01', end_date='2022-12-31';</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE PolicyHolder (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50),
    age INT,
    policy_type VARCHAR(20),
    policy_amount DECIMAL
);


CREATE TABLE InsuranceCompany (
    company_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    company_name VARCHAR(50),
    location VARCHAR(50),
    contact_number VARCHAR(15)
);


CREATE TABLE Policy (
    policy_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    holder_id UUID REFERENCES PolicyHolder(id),
    company_id UUID REFERENCES InsuranceCompany(company_id),
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    premium DECIMAL
);
</t><s>UPSERT INTO PolicyHolder (id, name, age, policy_type, policy_amount) VALUES ('502b3590-6075-4e09-9749-ceb34c8aae3d', 'Alice', 35, 'Life', 10000.50) ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name='Alice', age=35, policy_type='Life', policy_amount=10000.50;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE PolicyHolder (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50),
    age INT,
    policy_type VARCHAR(20),
    policy_amount DECIMAL
);


CREATE TABLE InsuranceCompany (
    company_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    company_name VARCHAR(50),
    location VARCHAR(50),
    contact_number VARCHAR(15)
);


CREATE TABLE Policy (
    policy_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    holder_id UUID REFERENCES PolicyHolder(id),
    company_id UUID REFERENCES InsuranceCompany(company_id),
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    premium DECIMAL
);
</t><s>upsert into policyholder (id, name, age, policy_type, policy_amount) values ('502b3590-6075-4e09-9749-ceb34c8aae3d', 'alice', 35, 'life', 10000.50) on conflict (id) do update set name='alice', age=35, policy_type='life', policy_amount=10000.50;</s>

CREATE TABLE Policies (id INT PRIMARY KEY, policy_number STRING, policy_type STRING, customer_id INT REFERENCES Customers(id))

CREATE TABLE Claims (id INT PRIMARY KEY, claim_number STRING, date DATE, amount FLOAT, customer_id INT REFERENCES Customers(id))
